   200 export async function getEntryByDate(date: string, gardenId?: number): Promise<Entry | null> {
   201   const db = await getDb();
   202   const active = gardenId ?? (await getActiveGarden()).id;
   203   const rows = await db.getAllAsync<Entry>('SELECT * FROM entries WHERE date = ? AND garden_id = ? LIMIT 1', [
   204     date,
   205     active,
   206   ]);
   207   return rows[0] ?? null;
   208 }
   209 
   210 export async function getEntriesForMonth(year: number, month: number, gardenId?: number): Promise<Entry[]> {
   211   const db = await getDb();
   212   const active = gardenId ?? (await getActiveGarden()).id;
   213   const start = `${year}-${String(month + 1).padStart(2, '0')}-01`;
   214   const nextMonth = month === 11 ? `${year + 1}-01-01` : `${year}-${String(month + 2).padStart(2, '0')}-01`;
   215   return db.getAllAsync<Entry>(
   216     'SELECT * FROM entries WHERE date >= ? AND date < ? AND garden_id = ? ORDER BY date ASC',
   217     [start, nextMonth, active]
   218   );
   219 }
   220 
   221 export async function getEntryCount(gardenId?: number): Promise<number> {
   222   const db = await getDb();
   223   const active = gardenId ?? (await getActiveGarden()).id;
   224   const rows = await db.getAllAsync<{ count: number }>(
   225     'SELECT COUNT(*) as count FROM entries WHERE garden_id = ?',
   226     [active]
   227   );
   228   return rows[0]?.count ?? 0;
   229 }

export function checkAchievements(params: {
  total: number;
  streak: number;
  uniqueMoods: Set<string>;
  gardenCount: number;
  favoriteCount: number;
  photoCount: number;
  customPromptCount: number;
  customMoodCount: number;
}): string[] {
  const unlocked: string[] = [];
  if (params.total >= 1) unlocked.push('first_entry');
  if (params.streak >= 3) unlocked.push('streak_3');
  if (params.streak >= 7) unlocked.push('streak_7');
  if (params.streak >= 30) unlocked.push('streak_30');
  if (params.total >= 10) unlocked.push('total_10');
  if (params.total >= 50) unlocked.push('total_50');
  if (params.total >= 100) unlocked.push('total_100');
  if (params.uniqueMoods.size >= 6) unlocked.push('all_moods');
  if (params.gardenCount >= 2) unlocked.push('second_garden');
  if (params.favoriteCount >= 1) unlocked.push('first_favorite');
  if (params.photoCount >= 1) unlocked.push('first_photo');
  if (params.customPromptCount >= 1) unlocked.push('first_custom_prompt');
  if (params.customMoodCount >= 1) unlocked.push('first_custom_mood');
  return unlocked;
}

export async function refreshAchievements(): Promise<string[]> {
  const [entries, gardens, favorites, customPrompts, customMoods] = await Promise.all([
    getAllEntries(),
    getGardens(),
    getFavoriteEntries(),

New String: ```
import {
  getAllEntries,
  getGardens,
  getFavoriteEntries,
  getCustomPrompts,
  getCustomMoods,
  unlockAchievement,
  getEntriesByGarden,
} from './database';
import { checkAchievements } from './achievements';
import { computeStats } from './stats';
import { todayString } from './date';
import { isGardenFull, GARDEN_CAPACITY } from './garden';

export async function refreshAchievements(): Promise<string[]> {
  const [entries, gardens, favorites, customPrompts, customMoods] = await Promise.all([
    getAllEntries(),
    getGardens(),
    getFavoriteEntries(),
    getCustomPrompts(),
    getCustomMoods(),
  ]);

  const uniqueMoods = new Set(entries.map((e) => e.mood_key));
  const photoCount = entries.filter((e) => e.image_uri).length;
  const noteCount = entries.filter((e) => e.note && e.note.trim().length > 0).length;
  const stats = computeStats(entries, todayString(), customMoods.map((m) => m.key));

  let hasFullGarden = false;
  for (const garden of gardens) {
    const gardenEntries = await getEntriesByGarden(garden.id);
    if (isGardenFull(gardenEntries)) {
      hasFullGarden = true;
      break;
    }
  }

  const keys = checkAchievements({
    total: entries.length,
    streak: stats.streak,
    uniqueMoods,
    gardenCount: gardens.length,
    favoriteCount: favorites.length,
    photoCount,
    customPromptCount: customPrompts.length,
    customMoodCount: customMoods.length,
    noteCount,
    hasFullGarden,
  });

```

Created File with Text:
```
import { View } from 'react-native';
import Animated, { FadeIn, useSharedValue, useAnimatedStyle, withRepeat, withTiming } from 'react-native-reanimated';
import Svg, { Circle, Ellipse, Path, Defs, RadialGradient, Stop, LinearGradient } from 'react-native-svg';
import type { MoodKey } from '@/lib/types';
import { MOODS } from '@/lib/moods';

type FlowerShape = 'bloom' | 'bud' | 'droopy' | 'star' | 'leafy';

const SHAPE_MAP: Record<string, FlowerShape> = {
  sunny: 'star',
  bright: 'star',
  hopeful: 'star',
  calm: 'leafy',
  peaceful: 'leafy',
  grateful: 'bloom',
  energized: 'bloom',
  focused: 'bloom',
  creative: 'bloom',
  uneasy: 'bud',
  confused: 'bud',
  tired: 'bud',
  heavy: 'droopy',
  sad: 'droopy',
  motivated: 'star',
};

interface FlowerRoseProps {
  moodKey: MoodKey;
  size?: number;
  animated?: boolean;
}

export function FlowerRose({ moodKey, size = 48, animated = true }: FlowerRoseProps) {
  const mood = MOODS[moodKey];
  const color = mood?.colorHex ?? '#94A3B8';
  const shape = (mood as { flower?: FlowerShape } | undefined)?.flower ?? SHAPE_MAP[moodKey] ?? 'bloom';

  const pulse = useSharedValue(1);
  if (animated) {
    pulse.value = withRepeat(
      withTiming(1.06, { duration: 1600 }),
      -1,
      true
    );
  }

  const animatedStyle = useAnimatedStyle(() => ({
    transform: [{ scale: pulse.value }],
  }));

  const Wrapper = animated ? Animated.View : View;

  return (
    <Wrapper
      entering={animated ? FadeIn.duration(600).springify() : undefined}
      className="items-center justify-center"
      style={animated ? animatedStyle : undefined}
    >
      <Svg width={size} height={size} viewBox="0 0 64 96">
        <Defs>
          <LinearGradient id={`stem-${moodKey}`} x1="0" y1="0" x2="0" y2="1">
            <Stop offset="0" stopColor="#34D399" stopOpacity={1} />
            <Stop offset="1" stopColor="#059669" stopOpacity={1} />
          </LinearGradient>
          <RadialGradient id={`center-${moodKey}`} cx="0.5" cy="0.5" r="0.5">
            <Stop offset="0" stopColor="#FFFFFF" stopOpacity={1} />
            <Stop offset="1" stopColor={color} stopOpacity={1} />
          </RadialGradient>
        </Defs>

        {/* Stem */}
        <Path d="M32 96 Q30 70 32 50" stroke={`url(#stem-${moodKey})`} strokeWidth="3" fill="none" />

        {/* Leaves */}
        <Ellipse cx="22" cy="76" rx="10" ry="4" fill="#34D399" transform="rotate(-25 22 76)" opacity={0.9} />
        <Ellipse cx="42" cy="66" rx="9" ry="3.5" fill="#22C55E" transform="rotate(25 42 66)" opacity={0.9} />

        {/* Outer petals */}
        {[0, 60, 120, 180, 240, 300].map((angle) => (
          <Ellipse
            key={`outer-${angle}`}
            cx="32"
            cy="36"
            rx="8"
            ry="18"
            fill={color}
            opacity={0.85}
            transform={`rotate(${angle} 32 36)`}
          />
        ))}

        {/* Inner petals */}
        {[30, 90, 150, 210, 270, 330].map((angle) => (
          <Ellipse
            key={`inner-${angle}`}
            cx="32"
            cy="36"
            rx="5"
            ry="12"
            fill={color}
            opacity={0.65}
            transform={`rotate(${angle} 32 36)`}
          />
        ))}

        {/* Flower center */}
        <Circle cx="32" cy="36" r="7" fill={`url(#center-${moodKey})`} />

        {/* Decorative stamen dots */}
        {[0, 72, 144, 216, 288].map((angle) => {
          const rad = (angle * Math.PI) / 180;
          const r = 3.5;
          return (
            <Circle
              key={`dot-${angle}`}
              cx={32 + r * Math.cos(rad)}
              cy={36 + r * Math.sin(rad)}
              r="1.2"
              fill="#FFFFFF"
              opacity={0.8}
            />
          );
        })}

        {/* Soft shadow */}
        <Ellipse cx="32" cy="92" rx="10" ry="2.5" fill="#000000" opacity={0.08} />
      </Svg>
    </Wrapper>
  );
}

```
import { View } from 'react-native';
import Animated, { FadeIn, useSharedValue, useAnimatedStyle, withRepeat, withTiming } from 'react-native-reanimated';
import Svg, { Circle, Ellipse, Defs, RadialGradient, Stop } from 'react-native-svg';
import type { MoodKey } from '@/lib/types';
import { MOODS } from '@/lib/moods';

type FlowerShape = 'bloom' | 'bud' | 'droopy' | 'star' | 'leafy';

const SHAPE_MAP: Record<string, FlowerShape> = {
  sunny: 'star',
  bright: 'star',
  hopeful: 'star',
  calm: 'leafy',
  peaceful: 'leafy',
  grateful: 'bloom',
  energized: 'bloom',
  focused: 'bloom',
  creative: 'bloom',
  uneasy: 'bud',
  confused: 'bud',
  tired: 'bud',
  heavy: 'droopy',
  sad: 'droopy',
  motivated: 'star',
};

interface FlowerRoseProps {
  moodKey: MoodKey;
  size?: number;
  animated?: boolean;
}

export function FlowerRose({ moodKey, size = 40, animated = true }: FlowerRoseProps) {
  const mood = MOODS[moodKey];
  const color = mood?.colorHex ?? '#94A3B8';
  const shape = (mood as { flower?: FlowerShape } | undefined)?.flower ?? SHAPE_MAP[moodKey] ?? 'bloom';

  const pulse = useSharedValue(1);
  if (animated) {
    pulse.value = withRepeat(
      withTiming(1.07, { duration: 1600 }),
      -1,
      true
    );
  }

  const animatedStyle = useAnimatedStyle(() => ({
    transform: [{ scale: pulse.value }],
  }));

  const Wrapper = animated ? Animated.View : View;

  const isDroopy = shape === 'droopy';
  const isBud = shape === 'bud';
  const centerY = isDroopy ? 28 : 24;
  const petalY = isDroopy ? 30 : 24;

  return (
    <Wrapper
      entering={animated ? FadeIn.duration(600).springify() : undefined}
      className="items-center justify-center"
      style={animated ? animatedStyle : undefined}
    >
      <Svg width={size} height={size} viewBox="0 0 48 48">
        <Defs>
          <RadialGradient id={`center-${moodKey}`} cx="0.5" cy="0.5" r="0.5">
            <Stop offset="0" stopColor="#FFFFFF" stopOpacity={1} />
            <Stop offset="1" stopColor={color} stopOpacity={1} />
          </RadialGradient>
        </Defs>

        {/* Soft drop shadow */}
        <Ellipse cx="24" cy="42" rx="9" ry="2.5" fill="#000000" opacity={0.06} />

        {shape === 'star' ? (
          <>
            {[0, 72, 144, 216, 288].map((angle) => (
              <Path
                key={angle}
                d="M24 6 L27 18 L38 18 L29 25 L32 37 L24 30 L16 37 L19 25 L10 18 L21 18 Z"
                fill={color}
                opacity={0.9}
                transform={`rotate(${angle} 24 24)`}
              />
            ))}
            <Circle cx="24" cy="24" r="6" fill={`url(#center-${moodKey})`} />
          </>
        ) : shape === 'bud' ? (
          <>
            <Path d="M24 10 C14 16, 14 32, 24 42 C34 32, 34 16, 24 10" fill={color} opacity={0.9} />
            <Path d="M24 10 C28 18, 20 30, 24 42" fill="none" stroke="#FFFFFF" strokeOpacity={0.35} strokeWidth="1.5" />
            <Ellipse cx="24" cy="16" rx="4" ry="6" fill={color} opacity={0.7} />
          </>
        ) : (
          <>
            {/* Outer petals */}
            {[0, 45, 90, 135, 180, 225, 270, 315].map((angle) => (
              <Ellipse
                key={`outer-${angle}`}
                cx="24"
                cy={petalY}
                rx="6.5"
                ry={isDroopy ? 12 : 14}
                fill={color}
                opacity={0.85}
                transform={`rotate(${angle} 24 ${petalY})`}
              />
            ))}
            {/* Inner petals */}
            {[22, 67, 112, 157, 202, 247, 292, 337].map((angle) => (
              <Ellipse
                key={`inner-${angle}`}
                cx="24"
                cy={petalY}
                rx="4"
                ry={isDroopy ? 7 : 9}
                fill={color}
                opacity={0.55}
                transform={`rotate(${angle} 24 ${petalY})`}
              />
            ))}
            <Circle cx="24" cy={centerY} r="6.5" fill={`url(#center-${moodKey})`} />
            {/* Stamen dots */}
            {[0, 72, 144, 216, 288].map((angle) => {
              const rad = (angle * Math.PI) / 180;
              const r = 3;
              return (
                <Circle
                  key={`dot-${angle}`}
                  cx={centerY + r * Math.cos(rad)}
                  cy={centerY + r * Math.sin(rad)}
                  r="1"
                  fill="#FFFFFF"
                  opacity={0.75}
                />
              );
            })}
          </>
        )}
      </Svg>
    </Wrapper>
  );
}
